                                                                                                                                               corporate banking general director at maritime bank, general director of vietnam international
                                                                                                                                               bank (vib), deputy general director and head of retail banking of vib, cfo of vib, cfo of oracle

sustainable development

          corporate culture


          at vingroup, we respect and maximise the potential of each individual. this process and responsibility is not only
          reflected by our care for employees' standard of living, but also activities that help develop a corporate community.
